\title{Bd. 10 - Frankls Vermutung}

\chapter{Einleitung}

Dieser Band ist ein eigenständiges Sammelbecken für die Mengen-, Quotienten-
und Halbverbandsformen von Frankls Vermutung. Die Vermutung selbst bleibt
klar von den vollständig bewiesenen Teilresultaten und Reduktionen getrennt.
Nur fachübergreifende Werkzeuge bleiben in ihren Grundlagenbänden: die
allgemeine Theorie von Mengenfamilien, Funktionen, Äquivalenzrelationen,
Ordnungen, Endlichkeit und Halbverbänden. Alle vermutungsspezifischen
Anwendungen dieser Werkzeuge werden hier zusammengeführt.

\chapter{Frankls Vermutung für Mengensysteme}

\section{Grundwerkzeuge für Frankl-Familien}

Die folgenden elementbezogenen Teilfamilien, ihre Endlichkeit und die
zugehörige Adjunktionsabbildung werden ausschließlich für die
Frankl-Theorie benötigt und deshalb in diesem Band gebündelt.

\subsection{Elementbezogene Teilfamilien}

Für eine Familie \(M\) und ein Element \(a\) zerlegen die folgenden beiden
Teilmengenfamilien \(M\) danach, ob ihre Elemente \(a\) enthalten oder
vermeiden.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Enthaltende Teilfamilie zu einem Element]{%
  \FamContaining{M}{a} \coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}
}{Enthaltende Teilfamilie}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\FamContaining{M}{a}}
}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Vermeidende Teilfamilie zu einem Element]{%
  \FamAvoiding{M}{a} \coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}
}{Vermeidende Teilfamilie}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
}

\FormulaThmDelta[Enthaltende Teilfamilie ist Teilfamilie]{%
  \FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M\land a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rAEa{2}}
  \proofstep{}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{1,3}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Vermeidende Teilfamilie ist Teilfamilie]{%
  \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rAEa{2}}
  \proofstep{}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{1,3}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Enthaltende Teilfamilie als relatives Komplement der vermeidenden Teilfamilie]{%
  M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\FamContaining{M}{a}
}{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplement}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung
  \(M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq\FamContaining{M}{a}\)]{%
    \vdash M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq\FamContaining{M}{a}
  }{%
    \vdash M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq\FamContaining{M}{a}
  }[FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplementSubsetForward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\land X\notin\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x \in A \setminus B \eqvdash x \in A \land x \notin B}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rAEa{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\notin\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rAEb{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{a\notin X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,5]{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{Vermeidende Teilfamilie}{\rAI{3,5}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,5]{\bot}{\rBI{6,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\neg(a\notin X)}{\rCI{5,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\in X}{\FormulaRefAuto{rDN}{8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\land a\in X}{\rAI{3,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{Enthaltende Teilfamilie}{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar{%
      M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq
      \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{1,11}}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung
  \(\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\)]{%
    \vdash \FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  }{%
    \vdash \FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  }[FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplementSubsetBackward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\land a\in X}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{Enthaltende Teilfamilie}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rAEa{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\in X}{\rAEb{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{Vermeidende Teilfamilie}{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{a\notin X}{\rAEb{6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,5]{\bot}{\rBI{4,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\notin\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rCI{5,8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\land X\notin\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rAI{3,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x \in A \setminus B \eqvdash x \in A \land x \notin B}{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar{%
      \FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq
      \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{1,11}}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar{%
      M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplementSubsetForward}}
    \proofstepwidestar{%
      \FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplementSubsetBackward}}
    \proofstepwidestar{M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B, B \subseteq A \vdash A = B}{1,2}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDelta[Außenstehende Mengen sind nicht enthaltend]{%
  A\notin M\vdash A\notin \FamContaining{M}{a}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep A\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamContaining{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{A\notin M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in M\land a\in A}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in M}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\bot}{\rBI{4,1}}
  \proofstep{1}{A\notin \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rCI{2,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Außenstehende Mengen sind nicht vermeidend]{%
  A\notin M\vdash A\notin \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep A\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{A\notin M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in M\land a\notin A}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{A\in M}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\bot}{\rBI{4,1}}
  \proofstep{1}{A\notin \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rCI{2,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Enthaltende Teilfamilie ist vereinigungsabgeschlossen]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\vdash \UnionClosedFam(\FamContaining{M}{a})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in M\land a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in M}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{2}{a\in X}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in M\land a\in Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in M}{\rAEa{7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X \in M \dsep Y \in M \vdash X \cup Y \in M}{5,8}}
  \proofstep{2}{a\in X\cup Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{z \in A \vdash z \in A \cup B}{6}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in M\land a\in X\cup Y}{\rAI{9,10}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{11}}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(\FamContaining{M}{a})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rUI{\rRI{2,\rRI{3,12}}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Zwei vermiedene Mengenbestandteile bleiben in der Vereinigung vermieden]{%
  a\notin X\dsep a\notin Y\vdash a\notin X\cup Y%
}{UnionNotMemberFromBoth}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{X\dsep Y\dsep a}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin X}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{a\notin Y}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{a\in X\cup Y}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{a\in X\lor a\in Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{z\in A\cup B \eqvdash z\in A\lor z\in B}{3}}
  \proofstep{5}{a\in X}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,5}{\bot}{\rBI{5,1}}
  \proofstep{7}{a\in Y}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2,7}{\bot}{\rBI{7,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\bot}{\rOE{4,5,6,7,8}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{a\notin X\cup Y}{\rCI{3,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Vermeidende Teilfamilie ist vereinigungsabgeschlossen]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\vdash \UnionClosedFam(\FamAvoiding{M}{a})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in M}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{2}{a\notin X}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in M\land a\notin Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in M}{\rAEa{7}}
  \proofstep{3}{a\notin Y}{\rAEb{7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X \in M \dsep Y \in M \vdash X \cup Y \in M}{5,8}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{a\notin X\cup Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{UnionNotMemberFromBoth}[thm]{6,9}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in M\land a\notin X\cup Y}{\rAI{10,11}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{12}}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(\FamAvoiding{M}{a})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rUI{\rRI{2,\rRI{3,13}}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Endlichkeit elementbezogener Teilfamilien}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Enthaltende Teilfamilie einer endlichen Familie ist endlich]{%
  \Finite{M}\vdash \Finite{\FamContaining{M}{a}}
}{FiniteContainingSubfamily}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamContaining{M}{a}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteSubset}[thm]{2,1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Vermeidende Teilfamilie einer endlichen Familie ist endlich]{%
  \Finite{M}\vdash \Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
}{FiniteAvoidingSubfamily}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteSubset}[thm]{2,1}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Die Adjunktionsabbildung einer Mengenfamilie}

Die zuvor eingeführten Teilfamilien \(\FamContaining{M}{a}\) und
\(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\) bilden den natürlichen Definitions- und Zielbereich
für die punktweise Adjunktion \(X\mapsto X\cup\{a\}\). Unter
Vereinigungsschließung und \(\{a\}\in M\) wird diese Vorschrift zu einer
Funktion zwischen den beiden Teilfamilien.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Funktionsvorschrift der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
  \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}
}{Funktionsvorschrift der Adjunktionsabbildung}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}

\FormulaThmDelta[Funktionsvorschrift der Adjunktionsabbildung ist injektiv]{%
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\dsep Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\dsep
  \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)\vdash X=Y
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin X}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{1}}}
  \proofstep{2}{a\notin Y}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{2}}}
  \proofstep{1}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
    \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)=Y\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
    \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{X\cup\{a\}=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{6}}
  \proofstep{1,3}{X\cup\{a\}=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{8,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a\}=Y\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{9,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X=Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin X\dsep a\notin Y\dsep X\cup\{a\}=Y\cup\{a\}\vdash X=Y}{4,5,10}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Typisierung der Funktionsvorschrift der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  \vdash \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\in \FamContaining{M}{a}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in M}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a\}\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X \in M \dsep Y \in M \vdash X \cup Y \in M}{5,2}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in X\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a \in A \cup \{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a\}\in M\land a\in X\cup\{a\}}{\rAI{6,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a\}\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{8}}
  \proofstep{3}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
    \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rIE{10,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Existenz der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash{}\\
    &\exists! J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}\,{}\\
    &\forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
      J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash
  \exists! J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}\,
  \forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{J}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\exists! J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}\,{}\\
      &\forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
      J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
    \end{aligned}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      x\in A\vdash t(x)\coloneq y \dsep x\in A\vdash t(x)\in B
      \exists! F\colon A\to B\,\forall x\in A\,F(x)=t(x)
    }{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
      \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}},%
      \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep
      X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
      \vdash \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\in \FamContaining{M}{a}}{1,2}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Adjunktionsabbildung zur Einermenge]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash
  \FranklAdj{M}{a}\coloneqq \iota J\Bigl(
    J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}
    \land
    \forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
      J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
  \Bigr)
}{Adjunktionsabbildung einer Mengenfamilie}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{J\dsep \FranklAdj{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
}

\FormulaThmDelta[Typisierung der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M
  \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \rAEa{\FormulaRefAuto{%
      \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash
      \FranklAdj{M}{a}\coloneqq \iota J\Bigl(
        J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}
        \land
        \forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
          J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
      \Bigr)
    }{1,2}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Werte der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
    \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{%
      \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash
      \FranklAdj{M}{a}\coloneqq \iota J\Bigl(
        J\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}
        \land
        \forall X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\,
          J(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)
      \Bigr)
    }{1,2}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{\rUE{4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Explizite Werte der Adjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep
    X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
    \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{3}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\vdash
    \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{\rIE{4,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Adjunktionsabbildung ist injektiv]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M
  \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M
    \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to \FamContaining{M}{a}}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{4}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\FranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,4}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep
    X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
    \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{1,2,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2,5}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\dsep
    X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
    \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{1,2,5}}
  \proofstep{1,2,4}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\FranklAdj{M}{a}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,4,6}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\FranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{9,6}}
  \proofstep{1,2,4,5,6}{\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{10,8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,4,5,6}{X=Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\dsep Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\dsep
    \tFranklAdj{M}{a}(X)=\tFranklAdj{M}{a}(Y)\vdash X=Y}{4,5,11}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{3,\rUI{\rRI{4,\rRI{5,\rRI{6,12}}}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\section{Frankl-Vermutung}

Die Frankl-Vermutung, benannt nach Péter Frankl, betrifft endliche
vereinigungsabgeschlossene Mengenfamilien. In der folgenden Formulierung ist
\(M\) eine Menge von Mengen.
Für ein Element \(a\) verwenden wir die zuvor eingeführte Zerlegung in die
Teilmengenfamilien \(\FamContaining{M}{a}\) und \(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\).

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Halbhäufiges Element einer endlichen Familie]{%
  \HalfOcc{a}{M}\coloneqq
  a\in\bigcup M\land
  \exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}
}{Halbhäufiges Element}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{\FamContaining{M}{a}\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\HalfOcc}
}

Für endliche \(M\) bedeutet \(\HalfOcc{a}{M}\), dass höchstens so
viele Mengen aus \(M\) das Element \(a\) vermeiden wie enthalten. Da
\(\FamContaining{M}{a}\) und \(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\) zusammen \(M\)
zerlegen, ist dies die
injektive Form der Aussage, dass \(a\) in mindestens der Hälfte der Mengen
aus \(M\) enthalten ist.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Frankl-Eigenschaft einer Familie]{%
  \Frankl{M}\coloneqq \exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}
}{Frankl-Eigenschaft}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\Frankl}
}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Voraussetzung der Frankl-Vermutung]{%
  \FranklFam{M}
}{Frankl-Familie}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{\textbf{Axiome}}{}
  \DeltaRow{Nichtleerheit}
           {M\neq\varnothing}
           [\parbox[t]{3cm}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\neq\varnothing \eqvdash \exists x\,(x \in A)}}]
  \DeltaRow{\makecell[l]{Nichtleerer\\ Träger}}
           {\bigcup M\neq\varnothing}
           [\parbox[t]{3cm}{%
             \FormulaRefAuto{\bigcup A \coloneq \iota C\Bigl(\forall x\;\bigl(x \in C \;\leftrightarrow\;\exists B\in A\,(x \in B)\bigr)\Bigr)}\\
             \FormulaRefAuto{A\neq\varnothing \eqvdash \exists x\,(x \in A)}}]
  \DeltaRow{Endlichkeit}
           {\Finite{M}}
           [\parbox[t]{3cm}{%
             \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteEqCardEquiv}[thm]}]
  \DeltaRow{\makecell[l]{Vereinigungs-\\ abschluss}}
           {\UnionClosedFam(M)}
           [\parbox[t]{3cm}{\FormulaRefAuto{Vereinigungsabgeschlossene Familie}}]
  \DeltaRow{\textbf{Neue Symbole}}{}
  \DeltaPrem{Frankl-Familien}{\FranklFam{M}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Familien sind nichtleer]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash M\neq\varnothing
}{FranklFamNonempty}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{M\neq\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Familien haben nichtleeren Träger]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \bigcup M\neq\varnothing
}{FranklFamCarrierNonempty}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\bigcup M\neq\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Familien sind endlich]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \Finite{M}
}{FranklFamFinite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Familien sind vereinigungsabgeschlossen]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \UnionClosedFam(M)
}{FranklFamUnionClosed}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{1}}
\end{tabproof}

Wegen der Bedingung \(a\in\bigcup M\) in der Definition von
\(\HalfOcc{a}{M}\) muss die Trägervereinigung nichtleer sein. Die
Frankl-Vermutung lautet in dieser Form daher:
\[
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \Frankl{M}.
\]
Ohne die Zusatzannahme \(\bigcup M\neq\varnothing\) wäre bereits
\(M=\{\varnothing\}\) ein Gegenbeispiel zur Formulierung, denn dann gibt es
kein \(a\in\bigcup M\). Die Aussage wird hier nicht als bewiesener Satz
verwendet. Wir zeigen zunächst einige einfache Spezialfälle.

\subsection{Fall einer enthaltenen Einermenge}

\FormulaThmDelta[Frankl-Vermutung bei enthaltener Einermenge]{%
  \Finite{M}\dsep \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M\vdash \Frankl{M}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\{a\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a\}\in M
    \vdash \FranklAdj{M}{a}\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{2,3}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rEI{4}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{3}{a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{3,6}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\HalfOcc{a}{M}\coloneqq
    a\in\bigcup M\land
    \exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rAI{7,5}}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{\rEI{8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Frankl{M}\coloneqq \exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{9}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Fall eines nichtleeren Durchschnitts}

Mit der Notation für Durchschnitte von Mengenfamilien kann der zweite
Spezialfall direkt als \(\bigcap M\neq\varnothing\) formuliert werden.

\FormulaThmDelta[Leere vermeidende Teilfamilie liefert Frankl]{%
  a\in\bigcup M\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\varnothing
  \vdash \Frankl{M}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{%
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\dsep \FamContaining{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\varnothing\colon\varnothing\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\varnothing\colon \varnothing\inj M}}
  \proofstep{2}{\varnothing\colon
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{2},3}}
  \proofstep{2}{%
    \exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj
    \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rEI{4}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\HalfOcc{a}{M}\coloneqq
    a\in\bigcup M\land
    \exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj
    \FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rAI{1,5}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{\rEI{6}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Frankl{M}\coloneqq
    \exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{7}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Frankl-Vermutung bei nichtleerem Durchschnitt]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\dsep
  \bigcap M\neq\varnothing\vdash \Frankl{M}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\bigcap M\neq\varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{M\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{\exists a\in\bigcap M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\neq\varnothing\vdash \exists x\in B}{2}}

  \proofstep{5}{a\in\bigcap M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,5}{a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{M\neq\varnothing \dsep a\in\bigcap M
    \vdash a\in\bigcup M}{3,5}}

  \proofstep{7}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{7}{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{7}}
  \proofstep{7}{X\in M}{\rAEa{8}}
  \proofstep{7}{a\notin X}{\rAEb{8}}
  \proofstep{1,5,7}{a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{M\neq\varnothing \dsep a\in\bigcap M \dsep
    X\in M \vdash a\in X}{3,5,9}}
  \proofstep{1,5,7}{\bot}{\rBI{11,10}}
  \proofstep{1,5}{X\notin \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rCI{7,12}}
  \proofstep{1,5}{\forall X\,X\notin \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rUI{13}}
  \proofstep{1,5}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\forall x\, x\notin A\vdash A=\varnothing}{14}}

  \proofstep{1,5}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\in\bigcup M\dsep
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}=\varnothing
    \vdash \Frankl{M}}{6,15}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{4,5,16}}
\end{tabproof}


\subsection{Fall einer enthaltenen Zweiermenge}

Wir betrachten nun den Fall, dass die Familie ein Glied \(\{a,b\}\)
enthält. Lokal zerlegen wir \(M\) nach dem Auftreten von \(a\) und \(b\):
\[
\begin{array}{c|cc}
 & b\text{ wird vermieden} & b\text{ wird enthalten}\\
\midrule
a\text{ vermieden} &
M_{00}=\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b} &
M_{01}=\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\\
a\text{ enthalten} &
M_{10}=\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b} &
M_{11}=\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}
\end{array}
\]
Die Abbildung \(X\mapsto X\cup\{a,b\}\) injiziert \(M_{00}\) in
\(M_{11}\). Die gemischten Klassen \(M_{01}\) und \(M_{10}\) sind als
Teilmengen von \(M\) endlich. Gibt es eine Injektion
\(M_{01}\to M_{10}\), so werden die beiden Zweige zu einer Injektion
\(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\to\FamContaining{M}{a}\) zusammengeführt; damit ist
\(a\) halbhäufig. Gibt es keine solche Injektion, liefert der Vergleich
endlicher Mengen eine Injektion \(M_{10}\to M_{01}\). Dann werden die
Zweige analog zu einer Injektion
\(\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\to\FamContaining{M}{b}\) zusammengeführt; damit ist
\(b\) halbhäufig.

\paragraph{Lokale Klassenrechnungen}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Zerlegung der \(a\)-vermeidenden Klassen im Zweierfall]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
  &=
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \cup
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairAvoidADecomp}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
    =
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap(M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b})\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SubsetRelativeComplementDecomp}{1}}
  \proofstep{}{M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b}=\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplement}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}
    =
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \rIE{3,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Disjunktheit der \(a\)-vermeidenden Zweige]{%
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \cap
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  =\varnothing
}{FranklPairAvoidADisjoint}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap(M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b})\bigr)
    =\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{RelativeComplementDecompDisjoint}}
  \proofstep{}{M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b}=\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplement}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    =\varnothing}{%
    \rIE{2,1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Zerlegung der \(a\)-enthaltenden Zielklassen]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  \FamContaining{M}{a}
  &=
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \cup
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairContainADecomp}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar{\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstepwidestar{\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstepwidestar{%
    M\setminus(M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b})
    =
    \FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{RelCompInvolutive}{2}}
  \proofstepwidestar{M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b}=\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplement}}
  \proofstepwidestar{M\setminus\FamContaining{M}{b}=\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{%
    \rIE{4,3}}
  \proofstepwide{\FamContaining{M}{a}}{=}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\\
    &\cup
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap(M\setminus\FamContaining{M}{b})\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SubsetRelativeComplementDecomp}{1}}
  \proofstepwide{\FamContaining{M}{a}}{=}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\\
    &\cup
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rIE{5,6}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Disjunktheit der \(a\)-enthaltenden Zielzweige]{%
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \cap
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  =\varnothing
}{FranklPairContainADisjoint}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar{\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstepwidestar{%
    M\setminus(M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b})
    =
    \FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{RelCompInvolutive}{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar{M\setminus\FamAvoiding{M}{b}=\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamContainingAsAvoidingRelativeComplement}}
  \proofstepwidestar{M\setminus\FamContaining{M}{b}=\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{%
    \rIE{3,2}}
  \proofstepwidestar{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    \Bigl[
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap(M\setminus\FamContaining{M}{b})\bigr)
    \Bigr]
    &=\varnothing
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{RelativeComplementDecompDisjoint}}
  \proofstepwidestar{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    \Bigl[
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \Bigr]
    &=\varnothing
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rIE{4,5}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Endlichkeit der Klasse \(M_{01}\)]{%
  \Finite{M}\vdash
  \Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}
}{FranklPairMixed01Finite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\subseteq M}}
  \proofstep{}{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\subseteq M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq M \vdash A\cap B\subseteq M}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteSubset}[thm]{3,1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gegeninjektion im negativen Mischklassenfall]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  &\Finite{M}\dsep
  \neg\exists F\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \inj
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \vdash{}\\
  &\exists G\colon
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \inj
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairMixedReverseInjection}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\neg\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairMixed01Finite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\cap\FamContaining{M}{a}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairMixed01Finite}{1}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \FamAvoiding{M}{b}\cap\FamContaining{M}{a}
    =
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \cap B = B \cap A}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}}{%
    \rIE{5,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists G\colon
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite{M}\dsep \Finite{N}\dsep
    \neg\exists F\colon M\inj N
    \vdash \exists G\colon N\inj M}{3,6,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Die Zweieradjunktion}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Funktionsvorschrift der Zweieradjunktion]{%
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\vdash
  t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a,b\}
}{FranklPairAdjTerm}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Funktionsvorschrift der Zweieradjunktion ist injektiv]{%
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\dsep
  Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\dsep
  t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(Y)\vdash X=Y
}{FranklPairAdjTermInjective}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in A}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in B}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in A}{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in B}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin X}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{4}}}
  \proofstep{1}{b\notin X}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{5}}}
  \proofstep{2}{a\notin Y}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{6}}}
  \proofstep{2}{b\notin Y}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{7}}}
  \proofstep{1}{X\cap\{a,b\}=\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{PairSetDisjointFromTwoAvoided}{8,9}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\cap\{a,b\}=\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{PairSetDisjointFromTwoAvoided}{10,11}}
  \proofstep{1}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=X\cup\{a,b\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTerm}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(Y)=Y\cup\{a,b\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTerm}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a,b\}=Y\cup\{a,b\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{14},3},15}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X=Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{UnionCancelDisjointRight}{12,13,16}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Typisierung der Zweieradjunktionsvorschrift]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\dsep
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}
  \vdash
  t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)\in
  \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}
}{FranklPairAdjTermTyped}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in A}{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in M}{%
    \rAEa{\FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{4}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a,b\}\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Vereinigungsabgeschlossene Familie}{1,5,2}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a \in \{a,b\}}}
  \proofstep{}{b\in\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{b \in \{a,b\}}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in X\cup\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{z \in B \vdash z \in A \cup B}{7}}
  \proofstep{}{b\in X\cup\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{z \in B \vdash z \in A \cup B}{8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a,b\}\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{\rAI{6,9}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a,b\}\in\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{\rAI{6,10}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{X\cup\{a,b\}\in
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x \in A \cap B \eqvdash x \in A \land x \in B}{\rAI{11,12}}}
  \proofstep{3}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=X\cup\{a,b\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTerm}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}{\rIE{14,13}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Existenz der Zweieradjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  &\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\vdash{}\\
  &\exists! U\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \to
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\,{}\\
  &\forall X\in
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,
  U(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairAdjExists}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{U}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=X\cup\{a,b\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTerm}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTermTyped}{1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{1}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\forall X\in
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,{}\\
    &t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=X\cup\{a,b\}
    \end{aligned}}{\rUI{\rRI{3,4}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\forall X\in
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,{}\\
    &t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}
    \end{aligned}}{\rUI{\rRI{3,5}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\exists! U\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \to
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\,{}\\
    &\forall X\in
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,
    U(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)
    \end{aligned}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      x\in A\vdash t(x)\coloneq y\dsep x\in A\vdash t(x)\in B
      \exists! F\colon A\to B\,\forall x\in A\,F(x)=t(x)}{6,7}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Zweieradjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  &\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\vdash{}\\
  &U_{M,a,b}\coloneqq \iota U\Bigl(
  U\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \to
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\land{}\\
  &\qquad
  \forall X\in
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,
  U(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)
  \Bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairAdjDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{U\dsep U_{M,a,b}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Zweieradjunktionsabbildung ist Funktion]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\vdash
  U_{M,a,b}\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \to
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
}{FranklPairAdjFunction}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{U_{M,a,b}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{U_{M,a,b}\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \to
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \rAEa{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjDef}{1,2}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Auswertung der Zweieradjunktionsabbildung]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\dsep
  X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}
  \vdash U_{M,a,b}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)
}{FranklPairAdjEval}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{U_{M,a,b}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\forall X\in
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\,{}\\
    &U_{M,a,b}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)
    \end{aligned}}{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjDef}{1,2}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{U_{M,a,b}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)}{\rRE{3,\rUE{4}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Zweieradjunktionsabbildung ist injektiv]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M
  \vdash
  U_{M,a,b}\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \inj
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
}{FranklPairAdjInjection}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{U_{M,a,b}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{U_{M,a,b}\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \to
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjFunction}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{4}{X\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{Y\in \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{U_{M,a,b}(X)=U_{M,a,b}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{U_{M,a,b}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjEval}{1,2,4}}
  \proofstep{5}{U_{M,a,b}(Y)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjEval}{1,2,5}}
  \proofstep{4}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=U_{M,a,b}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{7}}
  \proofstep{4,6}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=U_{M,a,b}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{9,6}}
  \proofstep{4,5,6}{t_{U_{M,a,b}}(X)=t_{U_{M,a,b}}(Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{10,8}}
  \proofstep{4,5,6}{X=Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjTermInjective}{4,5,11}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{U_{M,a,b}\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{3,\rUI{\rRI{4,\rRI{5,\rRI{6,12}}}}}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Zusammenführung der Zweige}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Positiver Mischklassenfall liefert Frankl]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  &\UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep \{a,b\}\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep{}\\
  &\exists F\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \inj
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \vdash \Frankl{M}
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairPositiveBranch}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep H\dsep U_{M,a,b}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{U_{M,a,b}\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAdjInjection}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{6}{F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    =\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAvoidADisjoint}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cap
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    =\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairContainADisjoint}}
  \proofstep{1,2,6}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\exists H\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\\
    &\inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \end{aligned}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{CaseFunDisjointTargetInjection}{7,8,5,6}}
  \proofstep{10}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &H\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)\\
    &\inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \end{aligned}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    =\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairAvoidADecomp}}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \cup
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    =\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairContainADecomp}}}
  \proofstep{10}{H\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \rIE{11,\rIE{12,10}}}
  \proofstep{3,10}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Frankl{M}\coloneqq \exists a\,\HalfOcc{a}{M}}{%
      \rEI{\FormulaRefAuto{\HalfOcc{a}{M}\coloneqq
        a\in\bigcup M\land
        \exists F\colon \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\inj \FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
          \rAI{3,\rEI{13}}}}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,6}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{9,10,14}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{4,6,15}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Negativer Mischklassenfall liefert Frankl]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
  &\Finite{M}\dsep \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep
  \{a,b\}\in M\dsep b\in\bigcup M\dsep{}\\
  &\neg\exists F\colon
  \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
  \inj
  \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
  \vdash \Frankl{M}
  \end{aligned}
}{FranklPairNegativeBranch}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{b\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{\neg\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,5}{\exists G\colon
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairMixedReverseInjection}{1,5}}
  \proofstep{7}{G\colon
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\{a,b\}=\{b,a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{\{a,b\} = \{b,a\}}}
  \proofstep{3}{\{b,a\}\in M}{\rIE{8,3}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}
    =
    \FamAvoiding{M}{b}\cap\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \cap B = B \cap A}}
  \proofstep{}{
    \FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}
    =
    \FamContaining{M}{b}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \cap B = B \cap A}}
  \proofstep{7}{G\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\cap\FamContaining{M}{a}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{b}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\bigr)}{%
    \rIE{11,\rIE{10,7}}}
  \proofstep{7}{\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\cap\FamContaining{M}{a}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{b}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\bigr)}{\rEI{12}}
  \proofstep{2,3,4,7}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairPositiveBranch}{2,9,4,13}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,5}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{6,7,14}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Vermutung bei enthaltener Zweiermenge]{%
  \Finite{M}\dsep \UnionClosedFam(M)\dsep a\neq b\dsep \{a,b\}\in M
  \vdash \Frankl{M}
}{FranklPairMemberFrankl}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{a\neq b}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{a\in\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a \in \{a,b\}}}
  \proofstep{}{b\in\{a,b\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{b \in \{a,b\}}}
  \proofstep{4}{a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{4,5}}
  \proofstep{4}{b\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{4,6}}
  \proofstep{}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)\\
    &{}\lor
    \neg\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \end{aligned}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P \lor \neg P}}

  \proofstep{10}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj\\
    &\bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)
    \end{aligned}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2,4,7,10}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairPositiveBranch}{2,4,7,10}}

  \proofstep{12}{\neg\exists F\colon
    \bigl(\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\cap\FamContaining{M}{b}\bigr)
    \inj
    \bigl(\FamContaining{M}{a}\cap\FamAvoiding{M}{b}\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,4,8,12}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairNegativeBranch}{1,2,4,8,12}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{\Frankl{M}}{\rOE{9,10,11,12,13}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Frankl-Familie mit enthaltener Zweiermenge erfüllt Frankl]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\dsep
  \exists a\,\exists b\,(a\neq b\land \{a,b\}\in M)
  \vdash \Frankl{M}
}{FranklFamPairMemberFrankl}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\exists a\,\exists b\,(a\neq b\land \{a,b\}\in M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamFinite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamUnionClosed}{1}}

  \proofstep{5}{\exists b\,(a\neq b\land \{a,b\}\in M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{a\neq b\land \{a,b\}\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{a\neq b}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{\{a,b\}\in M}{\rAEb{6}}
  \proofstep{1,6}{\Frankl{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklPairMemberFrankl}{3,4,7,8}}
  \proofstep{1,5}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{5,6,9}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Frankl{M}}{\rEE{2,5,10}}
\end{tabproof}


\subsection{Reduktion auf endliche Mengenglieder über den
Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten}

Der folgende Abschnitt ersetzt die ursprüngliche Familie \(M\) durch eine
Quotientenfamilie, in der Elemente mit demselben Auftreten in \(M\)
identifiziert werden. Die allgemeinen Abbildungen, die dafür benötigt werden,
wurden bereits im Kapitel über Beispiele von Funktionen eingeführt:
die Quotientenbildabbildung \(\QuotFamMap{A}{R}{M}\) und die
Spurabbildung \(\TraceMap{F}\). Hier werden diese Konstruktionen nur noch auf
die Auftretensrelation von \(M\) spezialisiert.

\paragraph{Beweisskizze}

\begingroup
\footnotesize
\[
\begin{array}{@{}c@{}}
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
a\sim_M b
\quad:\Longleftrightarrow\quad
\forall X\in M\,(a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X)
\\[-.1ex]
\SameOccRel{M}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\OccClass{M}{a}=[a]_{\SameOccRel{M}},
\qquad
\OccQuotCarrier{M}=(\bigcup M)/{\SameOccRel{M}}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\OccQuotMap{M}
=\QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}
\colon M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})
\\[-.1ex]
X\longmapsto
\{\OccClass{M}{a}\mid a\in X\}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\OccQuotFam{M}=\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\OccQuotTraceMap{M}
=\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}
\colon \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)
\\[-.1ex]
C\longmapsto
\{X\in M\mid C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\text{ ist injektiv}
\quad\Longrightarrow\quad
\FranklFam{M}\vdash \Finite{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
\\[-.1ex]
\Longrightarrow\quad
Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}\vdash \Finite{Y}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\FranklFam{M}\vdash \FranklFam{\OccQuotFam{M}},
\qquad
\Frankl{\OccQuotFam{M}}\vdash \Frankl{M}
\end{array}}
\\[1.1ex]
\Downarrow
\\[-.2ex]
\boxed{
\begin{array}{c}
\text{Um die Frankl-Vermutung zu zeigen, genügt es,}\\
\text{Frankl-Familien mit endlichen Mengengliedern zu betrachten.}
\end{array}}
\end{array}
\]
\endgroup

\paragraph{Aufbau des Abschnitts}

Der Abschnitt beginnt mit den Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen, also mit den
Klassen von Elementen, die in allen Familiengliedern gleich auftreten. Danach
werden der Quotiententräger und die Quotientenabbildung aufgebaut. Die
anschließende Charakterisierung von \(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\) beschreibt die
Elemente eines Quotientenbildes durch Repräsentanten aus \(X\). Der
Mitgliedschaftstransport übersetzt dann \(a\in X\) in die entsprechende Aussage
\(\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\). Darauf folgen die Trennung der
Familienglieder und die Erhaltung von Vereinigungen. Die Spurabbildung kodiert
anschließend Quotientenklassen durch ihr Auftreten in den Familiengliedern von
\(M\) und liefert die spätere Endlichkeitsaussage. Am Ende werden die
Frankl-Eigenschaft zurück nach \(M\) transportiert und der Reduktionssatz auf
Familien mit endlichen Mengengliedern formuliert.

In einem kleinen Beispiel \(M=\{\varnothing,\{a,b\}\}\) treten \(a\) und
\(b\) in genau denselben Familiengliedern auf. Der Quotient ersetzt daher die
beiden Elemente durch eine einzige Klasse \(C=\OccClass{M}{a}
=\OccClass{M}{b}\), und die Quotientenfamilie hat die Form
\(\{\varnothing,\{C\}\}\). Der Quotient verändert also nicht die
Inzidenzstruktur der Familienglieder, sondern nur die Namen der Elemente.

\subsubsection{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}

Der erste technische Block stellt die Klassen bereit, die später die Elemente
des Quotienten bilden. Verwendet wird die bereits eingeführte
Ununterscheidbarkeitsrelation; neu ist hier nur ihre Anwendung auf den Träger
\(\bigcup M\). Die folgenden Sätze halten fest, wie diese Klassen über die
Relation gelesen werden und wann zwei Repräsentanten dieselbe Klasse bestimmen.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsklasse]{%
  a\in\bigcup M\vdash
  \OccClass{M}{a}\coloneqq
  \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}
}{OccClassDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Äquivalenzklassen}{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Charakterisierung der Ununterscheidbarkeitsklasse]{%
  a\in\bigcup M
  \vdash
  b\in \OccClass{M}{a}
  \leftrightarrow
  b\in\bigcup M\land (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}
}{OccClassChar}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{b\in \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}
    \leftrightarrow b\in\bigcup M\land (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{EqClassChar}{2,1}}
  \proofstep{1}{b\in \OccClass{M}{a}
    \leftrightarrow b\in\bigcup M\land (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{\rIE{3,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbare Elemente haben dieselbe Ununterscheidbarkeitsklasse]{%
  a\in\bigcup M\dsep b\in\bigcup M\dsep (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}
  \vdash
  \OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}
}{OccClassEqualFromRel}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{b\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{(a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{\OccClass{M}{b}=\EqClass{b}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}=\EqClass{b}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{EqClassEqualFromRel}{4,1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\OccClass{M}{a}=\EqClass{b}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\rIE{5,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rIE{6,8}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gleiche Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen liefern Ununterscheidbarkeit]{%
  a\in\bigcup M\dsep b\in\bigcup M\dsep
  \OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}
  \vdash
  (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}
}{OccClassRelFromEqual}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{b\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{\OccClass{M}{b}=\EqClass{b}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rIE{5,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}=\EqClass{b}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\rIE{6,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{(a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{EqClassRelFromEqual}{4,1,2,8}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsubsection{Der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient}

Dieser Block baut aus den Klassen den Quotiententräger und anschließend die
Quotientenabbildung auf. Die Abbildung ist eine Spezialisierung der allgemeinen
Quotientenbildabbildung aus dem Funktionskapitel. Die Beweise sichern zunächst
die Typisierung, bevor Eigenschaften der Bilder verwendet werden.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Träger des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  \OccQuotCarrier{M}\coloneqq
  \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}
}{OccQuotCarrierDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen liegen im Quotiententräger]{%
  a\in\bigcup M\vdash \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}
}{OccClassInCarrier}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}\in
    \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{EqClassInQuotient}{2,1}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}=
    \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierDef}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}\in
    \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}}{\rIE{3,4}}
  \proofstep{}{\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}=
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{5}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rIE{7,6}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Elemente des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotiententrägers besitzen Repräsentanten]{%
  C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\vdash
  \exists a\in\bigcup M\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}
}{OccQuotCarrierRepresentative}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotCarrier{M}=
    \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierDef}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\in
    \QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}}{\rIE{3,1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists a\in\bigcup M\,
    C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{QuotientRepresentative}{2,4}}

  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in\bigcup M\land
    C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\rAEb{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}
    =\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{8,10}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in\bigcup M\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \rAI{7,11}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\exists a\in\bigcup M\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \rEI{12}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists a\in\bigcup M\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \rEE{5,6,13}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\coloneqq
  \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}
}{OccQuotMapDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}\dsep
  \OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Typisierung der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung in die Potenzmenge]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})
}{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{}{M\subseteq\powerset(\bigcup M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamilySubsetPowerUnion}}
  \proofstep{}{\QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{QuotFamMapFunction}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}=
    \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapDef}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}})}{%
    \rIE{4,3}}
  \proofstep{}{\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}=
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierDef}}}
  \proofstep{}{\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}
    \subseteq \OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A=B\vdash A\subseteq B}{6}}
  \proofstep{}{\powerset(\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}})
    \subseteq \powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \vdash \powerset(A) \subseteq \powerset(B)}{7}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep B\subseteq C\vdash F\colon A\to C}{5,8}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Wert der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung]{%
  X\in M\vdash
  \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=
  \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}(X)
}{OccQuotMapValue}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep
  \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}=
    \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapDef}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=
    \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\dsep F=G\vdash F(x)=G(x)}{1,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Charakterisierung der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung}

Der folgende Block beschreibt die Werte der Quotientenabbildung elementweise.
Entscheidend ist, dass ein Element eines Quotientenbildes genau eine
Ununterscheidbarkeitsklasse mit einem Repräsentanten aus dem ursprünglichen
Familienglied ist. Diese Charakterisierung wird im weiteren Abschnitt mehrfach
als technische Brücke zwischen \(M\) und \(\OccQuotFam{M}\) benutzt.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen auf Familiengliedern]{%
  X\in M
  \vdash
  \forall a\in X\,
  \OccClass{M}{a}=
  \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}
}{OccClassesOnMember}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{a\in X}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassDef}{3}}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall a\in X\,
    \OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{\rUI{\rRI{2,4}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Bilder der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung liegen im Träger]{%
  X\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
  \vdash C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}
}{OccQuotMapImageInCarrier}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{3,1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\subseteq\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{4}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B,\, x\in A \vdash x\in B}{5,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Charakterisierung der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung]{%
  X\in M\vdash
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
    \leftrightarrow{}&
    C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land{}\\
    &\exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}
  \end{aligned}
}{OccQuotMapChar}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep
  \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\EqRel{\SameOccRel{M},\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelEqRel}}
  \proofstep{}{M\subseteq\powerset(\bigcup M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FamilySubsetPowerUnion}}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in
    \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{QuotFamMapChar}{2,3,1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=
    \QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapValue}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\QuotFamMap{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}{M}(X)=
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{5}}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}\bigr)}{%
    \rIE{6,4}}
  \proofstep{}{\QuotientSet{\bigcup M}{\SameOccRel{M}}=
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierDef}}}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}\bigr)}{%
    \rIE{8,7}}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall a\in X\,
    \OccClass{M}{a}=
    \EqClass{a}{\SameOccRel{M}}{\bigcup M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassesOnMember}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}\bigr)}{%
    \rIE{10,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Klassenzeugen liefern Bilder der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung]{%
  X\in M\dsep \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}
  \vdash C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
}{OccQuotClassWitnessToMap}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{\exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in X\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in X}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{1,4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassInCarrier}{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccClass{M}{a}=C}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{5}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rIE{8,7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAI{9,2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, Q \vdash P}{11,10}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rEE{2,3,12}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Bilder der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung liefern Klassenzeugen]{%
  X\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
  \vdash \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}
}{OccQuotMapImageClassWitness}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    \bigl(C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
    \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, P \vdash Q}{3,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Mengenfamilie]{%
  \OccQuotFam{M}\coloneqq \OccQuotMap{M}[M]
}{OccQuotFamDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\OccQuotFam{M}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Definitionale Charakterisierung des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}\eqvdash Y\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]
}{OccQuotFamDefChar}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep Y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofsplit}
\proofpart{\(\vdash\)}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotFam{M}\coloneqq \OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamDef}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{\rIE{1,2}}
\closeproofpart

\proofpart{\(\dashv\)}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotFam{M}\coloneqq \OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamDef}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}[M]=\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rIE{3,2}}
\closeproofpart
\end{tabproofsplit}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Charakterisierung des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}
  \eqvdash
  Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\land
  \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
}{OccQuotFamChar}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
\proofpartwide{\(\vdash\)}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamDefChar}{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotMap{M}[M]\subseteq
    \powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B \vdash F[A]\subseteq B}{3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\dsep x\in A\vdash x\in B}{4,2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep y\in F[A]\vdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{3,2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\land
    \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAI{5,6}}
\closeproofpartwide

\proofpartwide{\(\dashv\)}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\land
    \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}

  \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in M\land Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in M}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{5,6}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{Y\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)\vdash y\in F[A]}{3,7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamDefChar}{8}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rEE{2,4,9}}
\closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

Wenn etwa die Elemente 1 und 2 durch die Familienglieder von \(M\) nicht
unterschieden werden, dann gilt \(\OccClass{M}{1}=\OccClass{M}{2}\). Das Familienglied
\(\{1,2,3,4\}\) wird im Quotienten durch die Klassen
\(\{\OccClass{M}{1},\OccClass{M}{3},\OccClass{M}{4}\}\) dargestellt; die
Klasse \(\OccClass{M}{1}\) kann informell als ein neues Element gelesen werden.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Typisierung der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\OccQuotFam{M}
}{OccQuotMapFunction}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{M\subseteq M}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq A}}
  \proofstep{2}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotMap{M}[M]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A\dsep F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in C\vdash F(x)\in F[C]}{3,1,2}}
  \proofstep{2}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamDefChar}{4}}
  \proofstep{}{\forall X\in M\,\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \rUI{\rRI{2,5}}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep \forall x\in A\,F(x)\in C\vdash F\colon A\to C}{1,6}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Wert der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung liegt im Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  X\in M
  \vdash
  \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}
}{OccQuotSetInFam}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapFunction}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{2,1}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Mitglieder des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten haben ein Urbild]{%
  Y\in \OccQuotFam{M}
  \vdash
  \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
}{OccQuotFamPreimage}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{Y\in \OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
