  \proofstep{1}{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\land
    \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamChar}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Mitglieder des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten liegen im Quotiententräger]{%
  Y\in \OccQuotFam{M}
  \vdash Y\subseteq\OccQuotCarrier{M}
}{OccQuotMemberSubsetCarrier}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep Y}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{Y\in \OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\land
    \exists X\in M\,Y=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamChar}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{Y\in\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{\rAEa{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{Y\subseteq\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{3}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Mitgliedschaftstransport}

Die nächste Aussage übersetzt eine Elementmitgliedschaft in einem
ursprünglichen Familienglied in eine Klassenmitgliedschaft im Quotientenbild.
Der Beweis zeigt beide Richtungen formal getrennt. Diese Übersetzung ist die
Grundlage für die späteren Trennungs- und Transportargumente.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Mitgliedschaftstransport in den Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  X\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M
  \vdash
  a\in X
  \leftrightarrow
  \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
}{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[\(\rightarrow\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M
    \vdash
    a\in X\rightarrow \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M
    \vdash
    a\in X\rightarrow \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
  }[OccQuotMembershipTransportForward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassInCarrier}{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rII}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in X\land \OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAI{3,5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\exists b\in X\,\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rEI{6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists b\in X\,\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rAI{4,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1,8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{a\in X\rightarrow
      \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rRI{3,9}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[\(\leftarrow\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M
    \vdash
    \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\rightarrow a\in X
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep a\in\bigcup M
    \vdash
    \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\rightarrow a\in X
  }[OccQuotMembershipTransportBackward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists b\in X\,\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\exists b\in X\,\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rAEb{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{b\in X\land \OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{b\in X}{\rAEa{6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,6]{b\in\bigcup M}{\FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{1,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rAEb{6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6]{(a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccClassRelFromEqual}{2,8,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6]{a\in\bigcup M\land b\in\bigcup M\land
      \forall Z\in M\,(a\in Z\leftrightarrow b\in Z)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelChar}{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X}{\rRE{1,\rUE{\rAEb{\rAEb{11}}}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6]{a\in X}{\FormulaRefAuto{P\leftrightarrow Q, Q \vdash P}{12,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{a\in X}{\rEE{5,6,13}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
      \rightarrow a\in X}{\rRI{3,14}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{a\in X\rightarrow
      \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransportForward}{1,2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
      \rightarrow a\in X}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransportBackward}{1,2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{a\in X\leftrightarrow
      \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rLRI{3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

Dieser Satz ist der zentrale Übersetzer zwischen der ursprünglichen Familie
\(M\) und der Quotientenfamilie. Er erlaubt, Aussagen über das Auftreten eines
Elements \(a\) in einem Familienglied \(X\) durch Aussagen über das Auftreten
der Klasse \(\OccClass{M}{a}\) im Quotientenbild zu ersetzen.

\paragraph{Trennung der Familienglieder}

Die nächste Aussage zeigt, dass die Quotientenabbildung auf den
Familiengliedern keine Information verliert. Wenn zwei Familienglieder dasselbe
Quotientenbild besitzen, dann stimmen sie bereits als Mengen überein. Der
formale Beweis wird über die beiden Teilmengenrichtungen geführt.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Quotientenbilder unterscheiden Familienglieder]{%
  X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep
  \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  \vdash X=Y
}{OccQuotSetSeparatesMembers}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\dsep \OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \(X\subseteq Y\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash X\subseteq Y
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash X\subseteq Y
  }[OccQuotSetSeparatesMembersSubsetForward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{a\in X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4]{a\in\bigcup M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{1,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{1,5,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3,4]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rIE{3,6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{a\in Y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{2,5,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{X\subseteq Y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq
      \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{4,8}}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \(Y\subseteq X\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash Y\subseteq X
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash Y\subseteq X
  }[OccQuotSetSeparatesMembersSubsetBackward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{Y\subseteq X}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetSeparatesMembersSubsetForward}{%
      2,1,\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{3}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{X\subseteq Y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetSeparatesMembersSubsetForward}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{Y\subseteq X}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetSeparatesMembersSubsetBackward}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{X=Y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B, B \subseteq A \vdash A = B}{4,5}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

Dadurch geht beim Übergang zum Quotienten kein Familienglied verloren und kein
Familienglied wird mit einem anderen zusammengelegt. Diese Trennung liefert
später die Injektivität der Quotientenabbildung auf \(M\).

\paragraph{Erhaltung von Vereinigungen}

Der folgende Block zeigt, dass Quotientenbilder mit der Vereinigung der
zugrunde liegenden Familienglieder verträglich sind. Der Beweis ist deshalb in
Fälle und zwei Teilmengenrichtungen gegliedert. Diese Eigenschaft wird danach
verwendet, um den Vereinigungsabschluss von \(M\) auf den Quotienten zu
übertragen.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Quotient erhält Vereinigungen]{%
  X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M
  \vdash
  \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  =
  \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
}{OccQuotPreservesUnion}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\dsep \OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(a\in X\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep
    a\in X\dsep C=\OccClass{M}{a}
    \vdash C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep
    a\in X\dsep C=\OccClass{M}{a}
    \vdash C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeftCaseX]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{\exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rEI{\rAI{3,4}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,4]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAI{2,5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1,6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{z \in A \vdash z \in A \cup B}{7}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(a\in Y\)]{%
    Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep
    a\in Y\dsep C=\OccClass{M}{a}
    \vdash C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }{%
    Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep
    a\in Y\dsep C=\OccClass{M}{a}
    \vdash C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeftCaseY]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in Y}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in
      \OccQuotMap{M}(Y)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeftCaseX}{1,2,3,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{%
      \OccQuotMap{M}(Y)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
      =
      \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \cup B = B \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in
      \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rIE{6,5}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \(\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\subseteq
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M
    \vdash
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\subseteq
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M
    \vdash
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\subseteq
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeft]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\cup Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists a\in X\cup Y\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{3,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rAEa{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{\exists a\in X\cup Y\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{a\in X\cup Y\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{a\in X\lor a\in Y}{\FormulaRefAuto{x \in A\cup B \eqvdash x\in A\lor x\in B}{\rAEa{8}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[11]{a\in X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3,4,8,11]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeftCaseX}{1,6,11,10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[13]{a\in Y}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,4,8,13]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeftCaseY}{2,6,13,10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,8]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rOE{9,11,12,13,14}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rEE{7,8,15}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\subseteq
      \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq
      \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{4,16}}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
    \vdash
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
    \vdash
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRightLeftCase]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{X\cup Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{1,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rAEa{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{\exists a\in X\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{a\in X\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{a\in X\cup Y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x \in A\cup B \eqvdash x\in A\lor x\in B}{\rOIa{\rAEa{7}}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{a\in X\cup Y\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAI{8,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{\exists a\in X\cup Y\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rEI{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3,7]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\land
      \exists a\in X\cup Y\,C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAI{5,11}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,7]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapChar}{2,12}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{\rEE{6,7,13}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)\)]{%
    Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }{%
    Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M\dsep C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \vdash
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRightRightCase]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{X\cup Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{Y\cup X=X\cup Y}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \cup B = B \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\cup X\in M}{%
      \rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{4},2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y\cup X)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRightLeftCase}{1,5,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{\rIE{4,6}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \subseteq \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\)]{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M
    \vdash
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \subseteq \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }{%
    X\in M\dsep Y\in M\dsep X\cup Y\in M
    \vdash
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
    \subseteq \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)
  }[OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRight]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\cup Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\lor C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x \in A\cup B \eqvdash x\in A\lor x\in B}{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,3,6]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRightLeftCase}{1,3,6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,8]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRightRightCase}{2,3,8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{\rOE{5,6,7,8,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
      \subseteq \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq
      \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{4,10}}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\cup Y\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\subseteq
      \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetLeft}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)
      \subseteq \OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnionSubsetRight}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)=
      \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B, B \subseteq A \vdash A = B}{4,5}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

Damit kann der Vereinigungsabschluss von \(M\) auf den Quotienten übertragen
werden. Die eigentliche Übertragung geschieht im nächsten Satz weiterhin in
einem vollständigen Tabellenbeweis.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Vereinigungsabschluss des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  \UnionClosedFam(M)
  \vdash
  \UnionClosedFam(\OccQuotFam{M})
}{OccQuotUnionClosed}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep U\dsep V}
  \DeltaRow{Quotientenbilder}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\dsep \OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{U\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{V\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{\exists X\in M\,U=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamPreimage}{2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\exists Y\in M\,V=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamPreimage}{3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M\land U=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[7]{Y\in M\land V=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[7]{Y\in M}{\rAEa{7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,6,7]{X\cup Y\in M}{\FormulaRefAuto{Vereinigungsabgeschlossene Familie}{1,8,9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6,7]{U\cup V=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rIE{\rAEb{6},\rAEb{7}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6,7]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\cup\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)=\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotPreservesUnion}{8,9,10}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,6,7]{U\cup V=\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)}{\FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{11,12}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,6,7]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X\cup Y)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetInFam}{10}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,6,7]{U\cup V\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rIE{13,14}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,6]{U\cup V\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rEE{5,7,15}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{U\cup V\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rEE{4,6,16}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\UnionClosedFam(\OccQuotFam{M})}{\FormulaRefAuto{Vereinigungsabgeschlossene Familie}{\rUI{\rRI{2,\rRI{3,17}}}}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\paragraph{Bijektivität der Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung}

Nach Trennung und Bilddefinition wird die Quotientenabbildung als Bijektion von
\(M\) auf ihr Bild \(\OccQuotFam{M}\) ausgewertet. Die Injektivität beruht auf
der Trennung der Familienglieder, die Surjektivität auf der Definition des
Bildes. Die Endlichkeit des Quotienten als Familie folgt anschließend aus
dieser Bijektion.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung ist injektiv]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\inj\OccQuotFam{M}
}{OccQuotMapInjective}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapFunction}}

  \proofstep{2}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=\OccQuotMap{M}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2,3,4}{X=Y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetSeparatesMembers}{2,3,4}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\inj\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{1,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung ist surjektiv]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\sur\OccQuotFam{M}
}{OccQuotMapSurjective}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\to\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapFunction}}

  \proofstep{2}{C\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\exists X\in M\,C=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamPreimage}{2}}
  \proofstep{4}{X\in M\land C=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{X\in M}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{C=\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=C}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b \vdash b = a}{6}}
  \proofstep{4}{\exists X\in M\,\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=C}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{5,7}}}
  \proofstep{2}{\exists X\in M\,\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=C}{\rEE{3,4,8}}
  \proofstep{}{\forall C\in\OccQuotFam{M}\,
    \exists X\in M\,\OccQuotMap{M}(X)=C}{\rUI{\rRI{2,9}}}

  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\sur\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Surjektive Funktion}{1,10}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotientenabbildung ist bijektiv]{%
  \OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\bij\OccQuotFam{M}
}{OccQuotMapBijective}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\inj\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapInjective}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\sur\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapSurjective}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\bij\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B\dsep F\colon A\sur B \vdash F\colon A\bij B}{1,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Endlichkeit des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  \Finite{M}\vdash \Finite{\OccQuotFam{M}}
}{OccQuotFamFinite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon M\bij\OccQuotFam{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapBijective}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotFam{M}}}{\FormulaRefAuto{FiniteBijectionTransport}[thm]{1,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Frankl-Familien unter dem Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten}

Dieser Block prüft die vier Bestandteile der Voraussetzung
\(\FranklFam{\OccQuotFam{M}}\) einzeln. Nichtleerheit, nichtleere Vereinigung,
Endlichkeit und Vereinigungsabschluss werden jeweils aus den entsprechenden
Eigenschaften von \(M\) gewonnen. Der abschließende Satz setzt diese vier
Bausteine wieder zur Frankl-Familie zusammen.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Frankl-Familie ist nichtleer]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing
}{OccQuotFamFranklFamNonempty}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{M\neq\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamNonempty}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists X\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\neq\varnothing\vdash \exists x\in B}{2}}
  \proofstep{4}{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetInFam}{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\vdash A\neq\varnothing}{5}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{\rEE{3,4,6}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Frankl-Familie hat nichtleere Vereinigung]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \bigcup\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing
}{OccQuotFamFranklFamCarrierNonempty}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\bigcup M\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamCarrierNonempty}{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists a\in\bigcup M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\neq\varnothing\vdash \exists x\in B}{2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\exists X\in M\,a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x \in \bigcup A \;\eqvdash\;\exists B\in A\,(x \in B)}{4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M\land a\in X}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in X}{\rAEb{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4,6]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{7,4,8}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetInFam}{7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4,6]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\bigcup\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\in A\dsep x\in B\vdash x \in \bigcup A}{10,9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\bigcup\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\vdash A\neq\varnothing}{\rEE{5,6,11}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\bigcup\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{\rEE{3,4,12}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Frankl-Familie ist endlich]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \Finite{\OccQuotFam{M}}
}{OccQuotFamFranklFamFinite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamFinite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotFam{M}}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamFinite}{2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Frankl-Familie ist vereinigungsabgeschlossen]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \UnionClosedFam(\OccQuotFam{M})
}{OccQuotFamFranklFamUnionClosed}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(M)}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamUnionClosed}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(\OccQuotFam{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotUnionClosed}{2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotient einer Frankl-Familie ist Frankl-Familie]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \FranklFam{\OccQuotFam{M}}
}{OccQuotFamFranklFam}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamFranklFamNonempty}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\bigcup\OccQuotFam{M}\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamFranklFamCarrierNonempty}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotFam{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamFranklFamFinite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\UnionClosedFam(\OccQuotFam{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotFamFranklFamUnionClosed}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{\OccQuotFam{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Frankl-Familie}{2,3,4,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsubsection{Transport der Frankl-Eigenschaft}

Der zweite Teil des Abschnitts arbeitet in die Gegenrichtung. Er zeigt, wie
Information aus dem Quotienten wieder auf die ursprüngliche Familie übertragen
wird. Dafür wird zuerst die Spurabbildung auf dem Quotiententräger verwendet;
danach werden vermeidende und enthaltende Teilfamilien entlang der
Quotientenabbildung verglichen.

\paragraph{Spurabbildung auf dem Quotiententräger}

Die Abbildung \(\OccQuotMap{M}\) ordnet einem Familienglied \(X\in M\)
sein Quotientenbild in \(\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})\) zu. Die
Spurabbildung \(\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\) ist die allgemeine Spur der
mengenwertigen Abbildung \(\OccQuotMap{M}\). Sie läuft in der
entgegengesetzten Inzidenzrichtung: Einer Quotientenklasse
\(C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\) ordnet sie die Familie aller \(X\in M\) zu,
deren Quotientenbild \(C\) enthält.

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Spurabbildung des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  \OccQuotTraceMap{M}\coloneqq
  \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}
}{OccQuotTraceMapDef}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep
  \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Neue Symbole}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Typisierung der Spurabbildung des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  \OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)
}{OccQuotTraceMapFunction}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstep{}{\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{TraceMapFunction}{1}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapDef}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)}{\rIE{3,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Wert der Spurabbildung des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten]{%
  C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\vdash
  \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
  \{X\in M\mid C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\}
}{OccQuotTraceMapValue}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstep{1}{\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)=
    \{X\in M\mid C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{TraceMapValue}{2,1}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapDef}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\dsep F=G\vdash F(x)=G(x)}{1,4}}
  \proofstep{1}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \{X\in M\mid C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{5,3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gleiche Quotientenspuren liefern gleiche Bildmitgliedschaften]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\\
    &\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)
    \dsep X\in M\\
    &\vdash
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)
  \end{aligned}
}{OccQuotTraceEqualityMembership}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotMap{M}\colon
    M\to\powerset(\OccQuotCarrier{M})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMapPowerFunction}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapDef}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\dsep F=G\vdash F(x)=G(x)}{1,6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(D)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\dsep F=G\vdash F(x)=G(x)}{2,6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{9,3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(C)=
    \TraceMap{\OccQuotMap{M}}(D)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{10,8}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{%
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{TraceMapEqualityMembership}{5,1,2,11,4}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gleiche Spuren vergleichen Repräsentanten punktweise]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep D=\OccClass{M}{b}\dsep
    a\in\bigcup M\dsep b\in\bigcup M\\
    &\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)
    \dsep X\in M\\
    &\vdash a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X
  \end{aligned}
}{OccQuotTraceRepresentativesMembership}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep
  \OccClass{M}{b}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{D=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{b\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[5]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassInCarrier}{3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rIE{1,7}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\OccClass{M}{b}\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassInCarrier}{4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2,4]{D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rIE{2,9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow
    \OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{6,3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,3,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rIE{1,11}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceEqualityMembership}{8,10,5,6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4,6]{b\in X\leftrightarrow
    \OccClass{M}{b}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{6,4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2,4,6]{b\in X\leftrightarrow
    D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rIE{2,14}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2,4,6]{D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\leftrightarrow
    b\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q \vdash Q \leftrightarrow P}{15}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow
    D\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P\leftrightarrow Q\dsep Q\leftrightarrow R
    \vdash P\leftrightarrow R}{12,13}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P\leftrightarrow Q\dsep Q\leftrightarrow R
    \vdash P\leftrightarrow R}{17,16}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gleiche Spuren vergleichen Repräsentanten]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep D=\OccClass{M}{b}\dsep
    a\in\bigcup M\dsep b\in\bigcup M\\
    &\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)\\
    &\vdash (a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}
  \end{aligned}
}{OccQuotTraceRepresentativesRel}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep X\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen}{\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep
  \OccClass{M}{b}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{D=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{b\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[5]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{X\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceRepresentativesMembership}{1,2,3,4,5,6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5]{%
    \forall X\in M\,(a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X)}{%
    \rUI{\rRI{6,7}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5]{%
    a\in\bigcup M\land b\in\bigcup M\land
    \forall X\in M\,(a\in X\leftrightarrow b\in X)}{%
    \rAI{3,\rAI{4,8}}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5]{(a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{SameOccRelChar}{9}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Gleiche Spuren trennen Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\dsep D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}\\
    &\dsep \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)
    \vdash C=D
  \end{aligned}
}{OccQuotTraceSeparatesClasses}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep a\dsep b}
  \DeltaRow{Relationen}{\SameOccRel{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\exists a\in\bigcup M\,
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierRepresentative}{1}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{\exists b\in\bigcup M\,
    D=\OccClass{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierRepresentative}{2}}

  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in\bigcup M\land C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rAEb{6}}

  \proofstepwidestar[9]{b\in\bigcup M\land D=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[9]{b\in\bigcup M}{\rAEa{9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[9]{D=\OccClass{M}{b}}{\rAEb{9}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,9]{(a,b)\in\SameOccRel{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceRepresentativesRel}{8,11,7,10,3}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,9]{\OccClass{M}{a}=\OccClass{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccClassEqualFromRel}{7,10,12}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,9]{C=\OccClass{M}{b}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, b = c \vdash a = c}{8,13}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,9]{C=D}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, c = b \vdash a = c}{14,11}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2,3,6]{C=D}{\rEE{5,9,15}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{C=D}{\rEE{4,6,16}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Spurabbildung auf dem Quotiententräger ist injektiv]{%
  \OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)
}{OccQuotTraceMapInjective}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapFunction}}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{C\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{D\in\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}(C)=
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}(D)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2,3,4]{C=D}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceSeparatesClasses}{2,3,4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{1,5}}
\end{tabproofwide}

Die Spurabbildung kodiert jede Quotientenklasse durch ihr Auftreten in den
Familiengliedern von \(M\). Ihre Injektivität ist der Grund dafür, dass der
Quotiententräger später als endlich nachgewiesen werden kann, sobald \(M\) eine
endliche Frankl-Familie ist.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Spurabbildung trennt Ununterscheidbarkeitsklassen]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash
  \exists T\colon \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)
}{OccQuotCarrierTraceInjection}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep C\dsep D\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{T}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[]{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapInjective}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{%
    \exists T\colon \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)}{\rEI{2}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\paragraph{Endlichkeit des Quotiententrägers}

Die nächsten Sätze verwenden die injektive Spur, um den Quotiententräger in
eine endliche Potenzmenge einzubetten. Daraus folgt zunächst die Endlichkeit von
\(\OccQuotCarrier{M}\), anschließend die Endlichkeit jedes Familienglieds des
Quotienten. Dieser Schritt ist der eigentliche Grund für die spätere Reduktion
auf Familien mit endlichen Mengengliedern.

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotiententräger ist endlich]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\vdash \Finite{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}{OccQuotCarrierFinite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{FranklFamFinite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\powerset(M)}}{\FormulaRefAuto{\Finite{A}\vdash \Finite{\powerset(A)}}{2}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\inj\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotTraceMapInjective}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\bij
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}[\OccQuotCarrier{M}]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B \vdash F\colon A\bij F[A]}{4}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}\colon
    \OccQuotCarrier{M}\to\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{4}}
  \proofstep{}{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}[\OccQuotCarrier{M}]
    \subseteq\powerset(M)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \dsep F\colon A\to B \vdash F[C]\subseteq B}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq A},6}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}[\OccQuotCarrier{M}]}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteSubset}[thm]{7,3}}
  \proofstep{}{{\OccQuotTraceMap{M}}^{-1}\colon
    \OccQuotTraceMap{M}[\OccQuotCarrier{M}]
    \bij\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B\vdash F^{-1}\colon B\bij A}{5}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{FiniteBijectionTransport}[thm]{8,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Glieder des Ununterscheidbarkeitsquotienten sind endlich]{%
  \FranklFam{M}\dsep Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}
  \vdash \Finite{Y}
}{OccQuotMembersFinite}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep Y}
  \DeltaRow{Quotiententräger}{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\FranklFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{Y\subseteq\OccQuotCarrier{M}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMemberSubsetCarrier}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite{\OccQuotCarrier{M}}}{\FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotCarrierFinite}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite{Y}}{\FormulaRefAuto{FiniteSubset}[thm]{3,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Vermeidende Quotientenmitgliedschaft]{%
  C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
  \vdash
  \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
  \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
  \leftrightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\bigr)
}{OccQuotAvoidingMembership}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C\dsep a}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{\OccQuotMap{M}}
  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{%
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\dsep \FamAvoiding{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[\(\rightarrow\)]{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\bigr)
  }{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\bigr)
  }[OccQuotAvoidingMembershipForward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}\land
    C\notin\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C\notin\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{a\in X}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,7]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{3,2,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,7]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rIE{1,8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,7]{\bot}{\rBI{9,6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{a\notin X}{\rCI{7,10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{\rAI{3,11}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rRI{4,12}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[\(\leftarrow\)]{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\bigr)
  }{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\bigr)
  }[OccQuotAvoidingMembershipBackward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in M\land a\notin X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{a\notin X}{\rAEb{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotSetInFam}{3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,8]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{1},8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,8]{a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{3,2,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,8]{\bot}{\rBI{10,6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{C\notin\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rCI{8,11}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\notin X\}}{\rAI{7,12}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}}{\rRI{4,13}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotAvoidingMembershipForward}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotAvoidingMembershipBackward}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamAvoiding{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \leftrightarrow X\in\FamAvoiding{M}{a}}{\rLRI{4,5}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaK[Enthaltende Quotientenmitgliedschaft]{%
  C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
  \vdash
  \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
  \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
  \leftrightarrow X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}\bigr)
}{OccQuotContainingMembership}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep X\dsep C\dsep a}

  \DeltaRow{Teilmengenfamilien}{%
    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\dsep \FamContaining{M}{a}}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[\(\rightarrow\)]{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}\bigr)
  }{%

    \vdash
    \bigl(\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in

    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}

    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{\OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in\OccQuotFam{M}\land
    C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{C\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{\rAEb{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
    \rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{1},6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,4]{a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{OccQuotMembershipTransport}{3,2,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{\rAI{3,8}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}
    \rightarrow X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rRI{4,9}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[\(\leftarrow\)]{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\bigr)
  }{%
    C=\OccClass{M}{a}\dsep a\in\bigcup M\dsep X\in M
    \vdash
    \bigl(X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}\rightarrow
    \OccQuotMap{M}(X)\in
    \FamContaining{\OccQuotFam{M}}{C}\bigr)
  }[OccQuotContainingMembershipBackward]
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C=\OccClass{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{a\in\bigcup M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{X\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in\FamContaining{M}{a}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{X\in M\land a\in X}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\FamContaining{M}{a}\coloneqq
    \{X\in M\mid a\in X\}}{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{a\in X}{\rAEb{5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,4]{\OccClass{M}{a}\in\OccQuotMap{M}(X)}{%
